# <a name="office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="224f9-104">21Vianet 運作的 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-104">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="224f9-p102">由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365，是設計用以滿足在中國對於安全性、可靠性和可調整性雲端服務的需求。這項服務由 Microsoft 授權給 21Vianet 的技術提供支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-p102">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet is designed to meet the needs for secure, reliable, and scalable cloud services in China. This service is powered by technology that Microsoft has licensed to 21Vianet.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-107">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-107">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="224f9-p103">Microsoft 不直接營運此項服務。由 21Vianet 營運、提供並管理服務的提供。21Vianet 是中國最大的運營商中立網際網路資料中心服務提供者，提供託管、受管理的網路服務，以及雲端運算基礎結構服務。透過 Microsoft 授權的技術，21Vianet 會營運當地的 Office 365 資料中心，以提供 Office 365 服務，並將資料保留在中國境內。21Vianet 也提供[訂閱和計費服務以及支援](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=847978
)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-p103">Microsoft does not operate the service itself. 21Vianet operates, provides, and manages delivery of the service. 21Vianet is the largest carrier-neutral Internet data center services provider in China, providing hosting, managed network services, and cloud computing infrastructure services. By licensing Microsoft technologies, 21Vianet operates local Office 365 datacenters to provide the ability to use Office 365 services while keeping data within China. 21Vianet also provides [subscription and billing services, as well as support](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=847978
).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
>  <span data-ttu-id="224f9-113">這些服務須遵守中國法律。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-113">These services are subject to Chinese laws.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="224f9-p104">由於中國服務的獨特本質 (由合作夥伴從中國內部的資料中心營運)，可能尚未啟用部分功能。經過一段時間後，客戶將會看到服務的功能逐漸完整。有關的差異，請參閱服務描述註腳。如需更高層級的差異概觀，請參閱[深入了解由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=846725)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-p104">Due to the unique nature of the China services—operated by a partner from datacenters inside China—there are some features that have not yet been enabled. Customers will see the services come closer to full feature parity over time. See the service description footnotes for differences. For a higher-level overview of differences, see [Learn about Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=846725).</span></span>
  
## <a name="service-availability-within-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="224f9-118">每個方案中可用的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-118">Service availability within each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="224f9-p105">每個由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 方案皆包含一些個別服務，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表顯示每項 Office 365 方案中可用的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-p105">Each Office 365 plan operated by 21Vianet includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-121">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-121">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="224f9-218">Azure 資訊保護</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-218">Azure Information Protection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-219">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-219">No</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-220">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-220">No</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-221">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-221">No</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-222">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-222">No</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-223">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-223">No</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-224">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-224">No</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-225">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-225">No</span></span>  <br/> |
   
> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-226"><sup>1</sup> 包含功能例如 Office 365 管理、Office 365 套件應用程式、使用者帳戶管理、網域、服務健康狀況和持續性、報告、服務更新、說明和訓練、網路等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-226"><sup>1</sup> Includes features such as Office 365 administration, Office 365 suite apps, user account management, domains, service health and continuity, reporting, service updates, help and training, networking, and so on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-227">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [平台功能](office-365-operated-by-21vianet.md#platform-features)表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-227">For more information, see the [Platform features](office-365-operated-by-21vianet.md#platform-features) table.</span></span>
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-228"><sup>2</sup> Project Online 並不包含在內，但可以當作附加服務來單獨購買，若是 Office 365 A1 方案，則可免費新增此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-228"><sup>2</sup> Project Online is not included, but can be purchased as a separate add-on service or added for free to the Office 365 A1 plan.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-229"><sup>3</sup> Visio Online 可以 （檢視功能） 是可用的可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-229"><sup>3</sup> Visio Online consumption (view capability) is available for free.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-230">Visio Online create and edit capabilities require a license.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-230">Visio Online create and edit capabilities require a license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-231">For more information about Visio Online, see the [Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-231">For more information about Visio Online, see the [Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1716"><sup>1</sup> 此版本的 Office 支援封存和相容性功能，但不包含 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online 方案，且必須另外購買或搭配支援的同等內部部署伺服器使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1716"><sup>1</sup> Archiving and compliance features are supported with this version of Office, but the Exchange Online and SharePoint Online plans are not included and must be purchased separately or used with supported on-premises server equivalents.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1717"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1717"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span>

 <br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1719"><sup>4</sup>商務基本 Skype 是供所有客戶使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1719"><sup>4</sup> Skype for Business Basic is available for all customers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1720">商務用 Skype 桌面用戶端是在本機安裝的應用程式，可針對包含 商務用 Skype Online 的 Office 365 方案，提供目前狀態、立即訊息和會議功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1720">The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1721">Office 365 專業增強版 和 Office 365 Enterprise E3 包含完整的 Skype 應用程式，其包含額外的功能，例如：進階電話語音支援、封存和法規遵循功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1721">Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1722">必須為每個使用者指派 商務用 Skype Online 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1722">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1723">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Skype for Business Online client comparison tables](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1723">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Skype for Business Online client comparison tables](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx).</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1724"><sup>5</sup> 部分學校符合教育增強版的資格，其包含 Office 365 專業增強版，可讓學生和教職員在最多五部 PC 或 Mac 電腦及其他行動裝置 (包含 Windows 平版電腦及 iPad) 上安裝最新版的 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1724"><sup>5</sup> Some schools are eligible for Education Plus, which includes Office 365 ProPlus, and allows students, faculty and staff to install the latest version of Office on up to five PC or Mac computers and on other mobile devices, including Windows tablets and the iPad.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1725">當學校透過註冊教育版解決方案、Open Value Subscription 教育版解決方案或學校合約，為全機構的教職人員授權 Office 時，學校即符合 Office 365 教育增強版的資格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1725">Schools qualify for Office 365 Education Plus when they license Office institution-wide for faculty and staff through Enrollment for Education Solutions, Open Value Subscription Education Solutions, or a school contract.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1726">請注意，Access 和 Publisher 僅在 PC 上可供使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1726">Note that Access and Publisher are available on PCs only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1727">Mac 版 OneNote 可分別從 Mac App Store 下載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1727">OneNote for Mac is available as a separate download from the Mac App Store.</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1729">Office 365 專業增強版支援<sup>7</sup>在使用者專用的虛擬桌面基礎結構 (VDI) 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1729"><sup>7</sup> Office 365 ProPlus is supported on user-dedicated virtual desktop infrastructure (VDI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1730">Office 365 當透過大量授權方案購買時，ProPlus 僅支援遠端桌面服務 (RDS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1730">Office 365 ProPlus only supports Remote Desktop Services (RDS) when purchased through a Volume Licensing Program.</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1736"><sup>10</sup> Visio Online 目前正由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 進行預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1736"><sup>10</sup> Visio Online is currently in preview for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1737">For more information about Visio Online, see the [Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1737">For more information about Visio Online, see the [Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1739"><sup>15</sup> Google 服務 （包括 Play 商店） 不是可從中國內部存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1739"><sup>15</sup> Google services (including Play Store) are not accessible inside China.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-1740">有數個應用程式儲存區維護的主要電話製造商或搜尋引擎公司，使用者可以在安裝來自行動應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1740">There are several app stores maintained by major phone manufacturers or search engine companies that users can install mobile apps from.</span></span>
  
## <a name="office-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="224f9-1741">Office Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-1741">Office Online features</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2699"><sup>1</sup> 郵件使用者會定義為「信箱」，而且可以連同外部郵件連絡人直接在 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 中新增、移除或管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2699"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2700"><sup>2</sup> 沒有 RBAC 自訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2700"><sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2701">僅限系統管理員角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2701">Admin roles only.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2702"><sup>3</sup> 在 EAC 中，可檢視受管理網域和編輯網域類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2702"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2703">其他所有網域管理作業都必須在 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2703">All other domain management must be done in the Microsoft 365 admin center.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2704"><sup>4</sup> EOP 與 Exchange Online 可用的彈性準則和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2704"><sup>4</sup> The available flexible criteria and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2705">如需 EOP 中可用的準則和動作清單，請參閱 [傳輸規則準則](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320392)和[傳輸規則動作](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320393)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2705">For a list of available criteria and actions in EOP, see [Transport Rule Criteria](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320392) and [Transport Rule Actions](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320393).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2706">如需 Exchange Online 中可用的準則和動作清單，請參閱[傳輸規則準則](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320394)和[傳輸規則動作](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320395)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2706">For a list of available criteria and actions in Exchange Online, see [Transport Rule Criteria](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320394) and [Transport Rule Actions](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320395).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2707"><sup>5</sup> EOP 稽核報告是 Exchange Online 稽核報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2707"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2708"><sup>6</sup> 預設的內容篩選動作，就是將垃圾郵件移至收件者的 [垃圾郵件] 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2708"><sup>6</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2709">若要讓此動作能在內部部署信箱中運作，您還必須在內部部署伺服器上設定兩個 Exchange 傳輸規則，以偵測 EOP 所新增的垃圾郵件標頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2709">For this to work with on-premises mailboxes, you must also configure two Exchange Transport rules on your on-premises servers to detect spam headers added by EOP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2710">如需詳細資訊，請參閱＜ [確定垃圾郵件路由傳送至每一個使用者的垃圾郵件資料夾](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320396)＞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2710">For more information, see [Ensure that Spam is Routed to Each User's Junk Email Folder](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320396).</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2711"><sup>7</sup> 透過 EOP 篩選其信箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客戶可以使用此功能，而且很快就可以供 Exchange Online 客戶使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2711"><sup>7</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2712"><sup>8</sup> EOP 報告是 Exchange Online 報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2712"><sup>8</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2713"><sup>9</sup> 包括 DLP 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2713"><sup>9</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2714"><sup>10</sup> 會掃描輸入及輸出郵件，但不掃描從組織中寄件者傳送給組織中收件者的內部郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2714"><sup>10</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2715"><sup>11</sup> EOP 與 Exchange Online 可用的述詞和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2715"><sup>11</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-2716"><sup>12</sup> 混合式安裝程式不能透過混合式精靈使用，但您可以手動設定 (如果您有 Exchange SP1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2716"><sup>12</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="224f9-2788">稽核</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2788">Auditing</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-2789">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2789">Yes</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="224f9-2790">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2790">Yes</span></span>  <br/> |
   
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="224f9-p136"><sup>1</sup> 使用者信箱必須位於 Exchange 2010 SP2 或更新版本上。 > <sup>2</sup>「就地封存」僅可用來封存已套用授權之單一使用者或實體的郵件。禁止使用「就地封存」來儲存來自多個使用者或實體的郵件。例如，IT 系統管理員不能建立共用信箱，再由使用者純粹為了封存的目的來複製 (透過 [副本] 或 [密件副本] 欄位，或透過傳輸規則) 共用信箱。 > <sup>3</sup> 如需支援的 Microsoft Outlook 版本清單，請參閱 [Exchange Online 封存中的用戶端功能](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md)。 > <sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。 > <sup>5</sup> 當您對信箱進行就地保留或訴訟資料暫留時，會同時保留主要和封存信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-p136"><sup>1</sup> User mailboxes must reside on Exchange 2010 SP2 or later. > <sup>2</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity for which a license has been applied. Using an In-Place Archive as a means to store mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited. For example, IT administrators can't create shared mailboxes and have users copy (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a transport rule) a shared mailbox for the explicit purpose of archiving. > <sup>3</sup> For a list of supported Microsoft Outlook versions see [Client Features in Exchange Online Archiving](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md). > <sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features. > <sup>5</sup> When you put a mailbox on In-Place Hold or Litigation Hold, the hold is placed on both the primary and the archive mailbox.</span></span> 
  
## <a name="sharepoint-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="224f9-2798">SharePoint Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2798">SharePoint Online features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="224f9-2799"><a name="BM8_SPOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-2799"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="224f9-p137">所有 Office 365 計劃都包括 SharePoint Online 服務，但並非所有計劃都支援所有的 SharePoint 功能。下表顯示計劃中是否提供某項功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-p137">All Office 365 plans include the SharePoint Online service, but not all plans support all SharePoint features. The following table shows whether a feature is available in a plan.</span></span>

## <a name="project-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="224f9-6020">Project Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-6020">Project Online features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="224f9-6022">下表列出可用於由 21Vianet 方案運作之 Office 365 的 Exchange Online 保護 (EOP) Project Online 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-6022">The following table lists the Project Online features that are available across Office 365 operated by 21Vianet plans.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]

## <a name="follow-on-wechat"></a><span data-ttu-id="224f9-6567">在 WeChat 上關注我們</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-6567">Follow on WeChat</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="224f9-6568"><a name="BM10_ProjectOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-6568"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="224f9-6569">掃描此 QR 碼，在 WeChat 上關注我們的討論區，並取得由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365 的最新更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="224f9-6569">Scan this QR code to follow discussions on WeChat and get the latest updates for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span>
